"If all 6.5 billion humans on Earth were programming, and every second, each one was producing code that was the equivalent of the entire Linux kernel history (1 million Git objects) and pushing it into one enormous Git repository, it would take 5 years until that repository contained enough objects to have a 50% probability of a single SHA-1 object collision. A higher probability exists that every member of your programming team will be attacked and killed by wolves in unrelated incidents on the same night."

Today is Facebook's 10th anniversary.
It's been an amazing journey so far, and I'm so grateful to be a part of it. It's rare to be able to touch so many people's lives, and I try to remind myself to make the most of every day and have the biggest impact I can.

ScienceAlert with Sushma Srivastava and 16 others.
If you fill two beakers with water, apply an electric voltage across them, and then separate them, you will form a water bridge. This phenomena was discover some 120 years ago and researchers believe it occurs because the voltage makes the water molecules line up, generating a dielectric tension...

ScienceAlert with Sushma Srivastava and 16 others.
If you fill two beakers with water, apply an electric voltage across them, and then separate them, you will form a water bridge. This phenomena was discover some 120 years ago and researchers believe it occurs because the voltage makes the water molecules line up, generating a dielectric tension...

Tolga Toleubay
Amazing thought-provoking painting "Beijing 2008" by Chinese-Canadian artist Liu Yi.
The woman with the tattoos on her back is China. On the left, focused intensely on the game, is Japan. The one with the shirt and head cocked to the side is America. Lying provocatively on the floor is Russia. And...

Shivam Chaturvedi
RT Amiya Shukla:
February 13 is celebrated as National Women's Day of India. This day is celebrated in the memory of Sarojini Naidu, the first Indian women governor, who was born on February 13. Sarojini Naidu ( 13 Feb 1879- 2 Mar 1949) was truly one of the gems of the 20th century India. Also known as the Nightingale of India, she was a child prodigy, Indian independence activist and poet.
Let us make India a better and safer place for our women and children. Happy Women's Day

Shivam Chaturvedi
IMPORTANT:
If you get a call or a missed call from any number beginning in +92 +22 or 37 etc. that you do not know of, PLEASE DO NOT PICK UP THE CALL OR CALL BACK THAT PERSON!!!
This is a scam which terrorists have been using to clone our SIM cards and then use your number for terrorist activities!
Do check the +91 before every unknown number that get a call from!
Share the news and Stay SAFE!
(To check this, search google for the same news and you'll get numerous articles concerning the same!)
